<body bgcolor="#ffffff" style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><br><br>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Exhibit
99.1</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><img src="acl6k0118sirionex9910.jpg" alt=""></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon
to Purchase Ophthalmic Pharmaceutical Assets from Sirion</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">HUENENBERG, Switzerland</font> <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#8211; January 18, 2010 &#8211; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Alcon</font> (NYSE: <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">ACL</font>), the world&#8217;s
leader in eye care, announced today that it will purchase the rights in the
United States for two FDA-approved topical eye care products from Sirion
Therapeutics, Inc.&#160;&#160;The two products purchased are Durezol&#8482;, a
marketed ophthalmic corticosteroid approved for the treatment of inflammation
and pain associated with eye surgery, and Zirgan&#8482;, a recently approved antiviral
for the treatment of acute herpetic keratitis (corneal ulcers).&#160;&#160;In
addition to these marketed products, Alcon also acquired the global rights,
excluding Latin America, for Zyclorin&#8482;.&#160;&#160;This product is currently in
clinical development to treat dry eye and other ocular surface
diseases.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>&#8220;The acquisition of these products from
Sirion is part of our business development strategy to gain access to late-stage
or approved products that will incrementally add to sales in the near-term,
while also building our long-term pipeline,&#8221; said Kevin Buehler, Alcon&#8217;s
president and chief executive officer.&#160;&#160;&#8220;Upon closing, this deal will
allow Alcon to capitalize on the U.S. registration approval for Durezol&#8482; and
Zirgan&#8482; with the existing commercial capability in the United States to maximize
the brand development and revenue opportunities.&#8221;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">"Durezol&#8482;
provides physicians with a steroid to treat both inflammation and pain following
a wide range of ophthalmic surgeries,&#8221; said Robert H. Osher, MD, professor of
ophthalmology at the University of Cincinnati College of Medicine and medical
director emeritus of the Cincinnati Eye Institute.&#160;&#160;&#8220;Physicians will
also appreciate the comfort and relief our patients receive for herpetic corneal
ulcers with Zirgan&#8482;, due to its low toxicity, potency and targeted antiviral
effect.&#8221;&#160;&#160;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
closing of this agreement is expected to occur by the end of the first quarter
of 2010 and is contingent upon customary closing conditions and required
regulatory approvals.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
Ocular Inflammation</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Cataracts
and glaucoma affect more than 24 million people age 40 and older in the United
States.&#160;&#160;Many of these people seek surgical treatment for these and
other eye conditions.&#160;&#160;Corticosteroids and non-steroidal
anti-inflammatory drugs are commonly used after eye surgery to manage
postoperative pain and inflammation.&#160;&#160;Complications can occur if
inflammation is left untreated and can interfere with a patient&#8217;s visual
rehabilitation.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
Durezol&#8482;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Durezol<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#8482;</font> (difluprednate ophthalmic
emulsion) 0.05% is a topical ophthalmic corticosteroid for the treatment of
postoperative inflammation and pain associated with ocular
surgery.&#160;&#160;Durezol&#8482; received approval from the U.S. Food and Drug
Administration (FDA) in 2008 and was the first ophthalmic steroid to be approved
for both postoperative inflammation and pain.&#160;&#160;Clinical trials
demonstrated that Durezol&#8482; </font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">- more
- -</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center">&#160;</div>
      <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
        <div id="FTR">
          <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
          </div>
        </div>
        <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
          </div>
          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
          </div>
        </div>
        <div id="HDR"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;</font></div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">reduced
ocular pain and inflammation rapidly and effectively for patients following
ocular surgery.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>Durezol<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#8482;</font> is a difluorinated
derivative of prednisolone and has anti-inflammatory activity.&#160;&#160;The
recommended dosing regimen for Durezol&#8482; is one drop four times daily beginning
24 hours after surgery and continuing throughout the first two weeks of the
postoperative period, followed by two times daily for a week and then tapering
off thereafter based on the response.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>The most common ocular adverse
reactions occurring in 5&#8211;15% of subjects in clinical studies with Durezol<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8482;</font> included corneal
edema, ciliary and conjunctival hyperemia, eye pain, photophobia, posterior
capsule opacification, anterior chamber cells, anterior chamber flare,
conjunctival edema and blepharitis.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
Zirgan&#8482;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Zirgan<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#8482;</font> (ganciclovir ophthalmic gel)
0.15% is indicated for topical ophthalmic use as a treatment for acute herpetic
keratitis (dendritic corneal ulcers).&#160;&#160;Zirgan&#8482; is an innovative
topical antiviral therapy designed to specifically target viral-infected cells
and has a low corneal toxicity profile, providing patients comfort and
relief.&#160;&#160;Zirgan&#8482; has been a leading treatment for corneal ulcers,
under the brand name Virgan<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font>, in
Europe for more than 10 years.&#160;&#160;The FDA also has designated Zirgan&#8482; as
an orphan drug, which is a special status for rare diseases or conditions that
affect fewer than 200,000 patients in the U.S.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
recommended dosing for Zirgan&#8482; is one drop five times per day until the ulcer
heals, and then one drop three times per day for seven days.&#160;&#160;The most
common adverse reactions reported in patients were blurred vision (60%), eye
irritation (20%), punctate keratitis (5%), and conjunctival hyperemia
(5%).&#160;&#160;Alcon anticipates Zirgan&#8482; to become available in the U.S. by
prescription in 2010.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">About Zyclorin</font>&#8482;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Zyclorin&#8482;
(cyclosporine) is a topical ophthalmic immunomodulator and immunosuppressive
agent.&#160;&#160;Zyclorin&#8482; is an investigational drug and is not approved by
the U.S. Food and Drug Administration.&#160;&#160;It is being studied for the
treatment of ocular surface diseases, including dry eye, which affects millions
of Americans.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
Alcon</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon,
Inc. is the world&#8217;s leading eye care company, with sales of approximately $6.3
billion in 2008.&#160;&#160;Alcon, which has been dedicated to the ophthalmic
industry for 65 years, researches, develops, manufactures and markets
pharmaceuticals, surgical equipment and devices, contacts lens solutions and
other vision care products that treat diseases, disorders and other conditions
of the eye.&#160;&#160;Alcon operates in 75 countries and sells products in 180
markets.&#160;&#160;For more information on Alcon, Inc., visit the Company&#8217;s web
site at <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.alcon.com</font>.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">J.P.
Morgan Securities, Inc. is acting as financial advisor and Proskauer Rose LLP is
acting as legal advisor to Sirion Therapeutics, Inc. with regards to the
transaction.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"># #

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">- more
- -</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center">&#160;</div>
